-----------------------Statements for SpikeCluster-------------------------

SpikeCluster is a software for extracting and classifying action potentials 
from different neurons. This utility is developed by Minggui Chen at Beijing 
Normal University. The first version was released on Mar 20th, 2012. It is 
for academic use only. Anyone who want to get SpikeCluster should contact 
the author directly (minggui.chen@gmail.com). Without permission, please do 
NOT distribute the program.

Minggui Chen
